# File: r_info.txt

# This file is used to initialize the "lib/raw/r_info.raw" file, which is
# used to initialize the "monster race" information for the Angband game.

# Do not modify this file unless you know exactly what you are doing,
# unless you wish to risk possible system crashes and broken savefiles.

# The format of a monster is as follows... ([] indicates an optional part)

# N:<monster index>:<monster name>
# G:<monster symbol>:<monster colour>
# I:<movement speed>:<attack speed>:<hit points>:<perception>:<armour class>:<sleep>
# W:<level found at>:<rarity>:<power>
# B:<attack type>[:<attack effect>][:<attack damage>]
# F:<flag1> | <flag2>...
# E:<information about special things which happen when the monster dies>
# [S:<spell frequency>]
# [S:<spell1> | <spell2>...]

# 'N' indicates the beginning of an entry. The serial number must
# increase for each new item. Entry 0 is used for the player.

# 'G' is for graphics - symbol and color. There are 16 colors, as
# follows:

# D - Dark Gray    w - White          s - Gray          o - Orange
# r - Red          g - Green          b - Blue          u - Brown
# d - Black        W - Light Gray     v - Violet        y - Yellow
# R - Light Red    G - Light Green    B - Light Blue    U - Light Brown

# (note that "black" is the same color as the screen background, and
# thus the monster will appear to be an empty black space if its
# color is "d".)

# 'I' is for information - movement speed (relative to normal speed, +10 is
# double speed, etc.), attack speed (blows per turn), health, vision in squares,
# armor class, and alertness. Alertness ranges from 0 (ever vigilant for
# intruders) to 255 (prefers to ignore intruders).

# 'W' is for more information - level, rarity, and relative power. A low
# positive rarity make the monster more common, but a rarity of 0 prevents
# generation altogether.
# Power controls whether a monster with either the KILL_BODY or MOVE_BODY flag
# can displace or destroy another given monster, affects the score bonus for
# killing one and has a few other minor effects.

# 'B' is for blows - method of attack, effect of attack, and damage
# from attack. There may be up to four of these lines; effect and
# damage are optional.

# 'E' is for death events. For further information, see lib/help/deathevent.txt.

# 'S' is for spells. The first S: line must be S:1_IN_X with X the
# number of monster turns, on average, before the monster will cast
# one of its spells. X must not be zero. If X is 1, the monster will
# never move while the player is in sight, and will thus never attack
# in melee, as it will cast spells every turn: if the monster is to use
# a melee attack, then X must be 2 or greater.

# 'F' is for flags. These are fairly self-explanatory. As many F:
# lines may be used as are needed to specify all the flags and flags
# are separated by the '|' symbol.

# 'D' is for description. As many D: lines may be used as are needed
# to describe the monster.

# === Understanding monster.txt flags ===

# UNIQUE monsters are just "special" monster races, with the requirement
# that only one monster of that race can exist at a time, and when it is
# killed, it can never again be generated.

# ATTR_CLEAR monsters appear the same color as the floor, terrain feature or
# object underneath them.

# ATTR_MULTI monsters are "multi-hued" - they change color, every player turn.

# CHAR_CLEAR monsters are totally invisible: the symbol shown on the screen
# is the same as the floor (or other terrain feature) below it, or the item
# that is lying on that floor. These monsters can currently be targetted as
# normal monsters: perhaps this can be changed so that the player must KNOW
# the monster is there (by bumping into it, or having the monster wake up
# and attack the player?)

# CHAR_MULTI monsters are those which look like objects, and use the symbols
# of objects. They are in plain sight, but the character should not know that
# a monster is there. At the moment, such monsters can be targetted normally
# (which means that this flag currently has no effect), but this may change
# in the future, as with CHAR_CLEAR monsters.

# (Note that currently both CHAR_CLEAR and CHAR_MULTI monsters are treated
# as normal monsters that are just a little hard to see... if you "l"ook
# for them, you will find them unless they are invisible and you cannot
# see invisible, and if you use the * command for targetting mode you
# can pick them as a target.)

# Version stamp (required)

V:1.0.15

##### Various causes of death #####

# The colour code for the @ fake monsters is as follows:
# w - probably your own fault.
# g - a slow death which probably indicates a lack of healing power. 
# y - a random event which you weren't healthy enough to survive.
# s - suicide.

##### Player ghost prototypes #####

# These are created from the files in lib/bone via a special generation routine.
# This means that several fields have an unusual meaning as follows:

# The name will always be preceded by the name of the character in the bones
# file. If it contains the word RACE, this is replaced by the race of that
# character.

# The hit dice and hit sides shown are multiplied by figures which give a
# ghost with roughly as many maximum hit points as the deceased character had.

# The experience is multiplied by an amount which increases with depth.

# A ghost type is chosen by picking a random level 1-12 levels deeper than the
# current one, and creating the deepest ghost prototype shallower than that
# level.
# This means that no two ghost prototypes should have the same depth, and there
# should be a ghost with depth 0.

# Rarity should always be 0 to prevent ghosts from being generated by other
# means.

# If a prototype has the TROLL or ORC flag, it will retain this flag if used
# in a bones file for a Half-Orc or Half-Troll character.

N:24:the Skeleton RACE
G:s:w
I:+0:2:1d1:100:26:0
W:0:0:100
B:HIT:HURT:2d6
F:ONLY_ITEM | DROP_GOOD | NO_SLEEP | NO_CONF | IM_POIS | COLD_BLOOD
F:EVIL | UNDEAD | UNIQUE | OPEN_DOOR | BASH_DOOR | IM_COLD | PLAYER_GHOST

D:in inconceivable, unlighted chambers beyond time amidst the muffled, 
D:maddening beating of vile drums and the thin monotonous whine of 
D:accursed flutes"
# H.P.Lovecraft: The Dream Quest of Unknown Kadath

### User-defined monster space ###

# Monsters which are placed after this point and given negative numbers are
# likely to be supported by future versions if the section of r_info.txt after
# this comment is copied without modification to r_info.txt for the new version.

# N:u1:& Boring monster~

# W:1:1:2
# B:HIT:HURT:1d1
